LIVE: Hegseth And Caine Hold Pentagon Press Briefing On The Iran War

Forbes Breaking News(5.5M)·39:06·15.4K views·2026-05-05
Pete HegsethSecretary of War Dan CaineChairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff
TL;DRThe Department of Defense has launched "Project Freedom," a defensive maritime operation led by U.S.
Central Command (CENTCOM) to secure the Strait of Hormuz, break Iran’s illegal blockade, and restore the free flow of global commerce. While a ceasefire remains in place,...

TL;DR

The Department of Defense has launched "Project Freedom," a defensive maritime operation led by U.S. Central Command (CENTCOM) to secure the Strait of Hormuz, break Iran’s illegal blockade, and restore the free flow of global commerce. While a ceasefire remains in place, the U.S. has established a "red, white, and blue dome" of protection over the waterway and warned Iran that any aggression will be met with overwhelming firepower.

Project Freedom: Scope and Objectives

  • Mission Profile: Secretary Pete Hegseth defined the operation as defensive in nature, focused in scope, and temporary in duration. It is distinct from the previous "Operation Epic Fury."
  • Primary Goal: To protect innocent commercial shipping from Iranian "extortion," including illegal tolling systems and harassment of civilian tankers.
  • Current Status: Two U.S. commercial ships and accompanying destroyers have already successfully transited the strait. Currently, 22,500 mariners and over 1,550 commercial vessels remain trapped in the Arabian Gulf awaiting safe passage.
  • Blockade Enforcement: While opening the strait for international commerce, the U.S. "ironclad blockade" against Iranian ports remains in full effect; six Iranian ships attempting to run the blockade were recently turned back.

Tactical Assets and Defensive Capabilities

  • "The Dome" of Protection: General Dan Caine reported that an enhanced security area has been established on the southern side of the strait, protected by a synchronized layer of land, naval, and air assets.
  • Force Composition:
      • Personnel: Over 15,000 American service members are currently dedicated to the mission.
      • Aviation: More than 100 fighters, attack aircraft, and drones provide 24/7 overwatch.
      • Command & Control: The 82nd Airborne Division is coordinating All-Domain Command and Control (JADC2) using AI-enabled tactical networks to synchronize effects across sea, air, and cyber domains.
  • Recent Engagements: Since the ceasefire was announced, Iran has attacked commercial vessels nine times and U.S. forces over ten times. U.S. Navy MH-60 and Army AH-64 Apache helicopters recently defeated Iranian cruise missiles, drones, and small boats targeting the strait.

Strategic Posture and Diplomacy

  • Ceasefire Status: Secretary Hegseth clarified that the ceasefire is not over, but described the U.S. military as "locked and loaded" to resume major combat operations if Iran escalates.
  • Nuclear Ambitions: The administration maintains that "Operation Midnight Hammer" successfully dismantled Iranian conventional capabilities and set back their nuclear program. Hegseth reiterated that the ultimate goal is a deal ensuring Iran never acquires a nuclear weapon.
  • Exit Strategy: The U.S. intends to hand over responsibility for the waterway to international partners. Hegseth noted that the "world needs this waterway a lot more than we do" and called on nations like South Korea, Japan, and Australia to assist in defending their own commercial interests.

Regional Threats and Allied Coordination

  • Iranian Aggression: Beyond the strait, Iran has recently targeted Oman once and the UAE three times, including an unsuccessful attack on the Fujairah oil terminal.
  • U.S.-Israel Alignment: Responding to questions about Israeli intent to collapse the Iranian government, Hegseth emphasized that while Israel is a capable partner, President Trump is "the only one hand on the wheel" directing U.S. strategy based on "America First" interests.
  • War Powers: Following the February 28 termination of formal hostilities, the administration views the 60-day War Powers clock as stopped, though the President retains the authority to restart operations if the ceasefire is breached.
"Iran is the clear aggressor, harassing civilian vessels, threatening mariners from every nation indiscriminately, and weaponizing a critical choke point for its own financial benefit... That ends with Project Freedom." — Secretary Pete Hegseth
"Commercial vessels that transit through the area will see, hear, and frankly feel U.S. combat power around them, on the sea, in the skies, and on the radio." — General Dan Caine
"We're not looking for a fight, but Iran also cannot be allowed to block innocent countries and their goods from an international waterway." — Secretary Pete Hegseth
"No adversary should mistake our current restraint with a lack of resolve." — General Dan Caine
As you know, President Trump has directed US Central Command to restart the free flow of commerce through the Strait of Hormuz under the umbrella of Project Freedom. To be clear, this operation is separate and distinct from Operation Epic Fury. Project Freedom is defensive in nature, focused in scope, and temporary in duration, with one mission: protecting innocent commercial shipping from Iranian aggression. American forces won't need to enter Iranian waters or airspace. It's not necessary. We're not looking for a fight, but Iran also cannot be allowed to block innocent countries and their goods from an international waterway. Iran is the clear aggressor, harassing civilian vessels, threatening mariners from every nation indiscriminately, and weaponizing a critical choke point for its own financial benefit, or at least trying to. For too long, Iran has been harassing ships, shooting at civilian tankers from all nations, and trying to impose a tolling system. Iran's plan, a form of international extortion, is unacceptable. That ends with Project Freedom. Two US commercial ships, along with American destroyers, have already safely transited the strait, showing the lane is clear. We know the Iranians are embarrassed by this fact. They said they controlled the strait. They do not. So, American ships led the way, commercial and military, shouldering the initial risk from the front, as Americans always do. And right now, hundreds more ships from nations around the world are lining up to transit. CENTCOM, along with partner nations, is in active communication with hundreds of ships, shipping companies, and insurers. All of these ships from all around the world want to get out of the Iranian trap that they have been stuck inside. As a direct gift from the United States to the world, we have established a powerful red, white, and blue dome over the strait. American destroyers are on station, supported by hundreds of fighter jets, helicopters, drones, and surveillance aircraft, providing 24/7 overwatch for peaceful commercial vessels—except Iran's, of course, which is why our ironclad blockade remains in full effect as well. In fact, six ships tried to run the blockade out of Iranian ports as Project Freedom commenced, and they were all turned around. This is more than strategy; it's also humanitarian. By breaking Iran's illegal stranglehold, we're protecting the lives and livelihoods of sailors from dozens of countries, securing global energy routes, and preventing shortages that hit the world's poorest people the hardest. Once again, America is using its strength to lift up others. Iran is trying to subjugate the world. To what remains of Iran's forces: if you attack American troops or innocent commercial shipping, you will face overwhelming and devastating American firepower. The President has been very clear about this. We prefer this to be a peaceful operation, but we are locked and loaded to defend our people, our ships, our aircraft, and this mission without hesitation. To Iran, let innocent ships pass freely. These international waters belong to all nations, not to Iran to tax, toll, or control. To our partners, allies, and the rest of the world, this is a temporary mission for us. As I've said before, the world needs this waterway a lot more than we do. We're stabilizing the situation so commerce can flow again, but we expect the world to step up. At the appropriate time and soon, we will hand responsibility back to you. To the incredible Americans executing this mission right now, simply thank you. Your courage, your readiness, your unmatched professionalism, and precision are why the world can breathe easier today and every day. You are and always will be the greatest fighting force in human history, unmatched, always. Project Freedom is underway, commerce will be flowing, and America is once again leading with strength, clarity, and purpose for the benefit of the entire world. Our will is unshakable. God bless our troops and God bless the mighty United States Navy as well. Mr. Chairman, over to you. Thank you, Mr. Secretary, and good morning everyone, and thanks for being here. On Sunday, at the direction of the President, CENTCOM initiated Project Freedom with the objective of facilitating the safe passage of international commercial shipping through the Strait of Hormuz. Over the past seven weeks, Iran has repeatedly threatened and attacked commercial shipping in the strait in order to effectively cut off commercial traffic and damage the global economy. By obstructing one of the world's most critical maritime choke points, a vital transit route for approximately one-fifth of the global oil consumption, Iran is weaponizing the global supply chain. This action disregards established navigational rights and the law of the sea, and the regime led by the IRGC is effectively attempting to hold the entire global economy hostage. Let me give you an update of the last few days of activity, and if you take a look at the map here, as the Secretary said, the United States has established Project Freedom to open up the Strait of Hormuz. This graphic highlights the kinetic engagements that the Iranians have attempted to make or have taken against the region. The green dots and blue dots show the groupings of commercial cargo and tanker vessels. The map shows the examples and samples of Iranian attacks against commercial vessels in the strait as well as the Gulf of Oman and up in the Arabian Gulf. They've attacked US forces more than ten times, all below the threshold of restarting major combat operations at this point. As a result of Iran's indiscriminate attacks across the region, there are currently 22,500 mariners embarked on more than 1,550 commercial vessels trapped in the Arabian Gulf, unable to transit. In addition to shipping, Iran has continued to deliberately attack its neighbors. As the Secretary said, Project Freedom is designed to protect commercial shipping and help restore the flow of commerce through the strait and sustain freedom of navigation. CENTCOM has established an enhanced security area on the southern side of the strait that is now protected by US land, naval, and air assets. I'd like to share a little bit more about US capabilities, but for operational security purposes, I'm not going to get into specific details out there. On the surface, guided missile destroyers and other warships are detecting and defeating Iranian threats. This includes fast boats and one-way attack drones. In the air, more than 100 fighters, attack aircraft, and other manned and unmanned aircraft are in the air 24 hours a day. As of this morning, as was mentioned prior, two US-flagged merchant vessels have transited and we anticipate more to transit over the coming days. Further up the gulf, US Naval Forces Central Command continues to work to identify and mitigate any threats. Beyond Project Freedom, CENTCOM and the rest of the joint force remain ready to resume major combat operations against Iran if ordered to do so. When the President or the Secretary need immediate, scalable, and lethal combat power in CENTCOM or elsewhere, the All-American Division answers the call. The 82nd is the core of our nation's immediate response force and ready to deploy within hours of notice. These paratroopers are capable of accomplishing any mission in any environment, constantly training, constantly ready to jump from Air Force aircraft into ground combat. They are ready to seize key terrain if ordered to do so, just like their predecessors did in Sicily and Normandy in World War II, or to secure or enable the follow-on forces to flow into theater as they did in Grenada or Panama. They can do the range of missions from counterinsurgency to counterterrorism operations to power projection as they have many times over the course of the history of this great division. They can do all these things because they're incredibly well-trained, well-equipped, and well-led, but also because of the indomitable spirit of the All-American paratrooper. Every single one of them volunteered for this role, volunteered to go to airborne training, and volunteered to serve. But this division is now more than just a formation that we use for forcible entries. For example, just today they are out there coordinating, integrating, and synchronizing land, air, space, sea, and cyber forces using All-Joint All-Domain Command and Control. They use next-generation tactical networks that are AI-enabled to augment intelligence and operations, and they seamlessly synchronize all of these effects and are doing so in support of Project Freedom as we speak. The relentless focus on technical innovation allows the commanders out there in the field to see, sense, and understand the opportunities that are in front of them along with the associated risks and make smart decisions out on the objective. With incredible courage, tenacity, and grit, they are going all the way every day, and whenever the nation calls on them, they are there to answer the call. Lastly, before I close as I often do, I want to remember some of our fallen. Today we remember Sergeant William Rivers, Specialist Brianna Moffatt, and Specialist Kennedy Sanders of the 718th Engineering Company, US Army Reserves out of Fort Benning, Georgia. They were tragically killed on January 28, 2024, when attacked by an Iranian-backed proxy force at Tower 22 in Jordan. We continue to carry on their memories. We remember their names, we remember their families, and the Secretary and I are deeply grateful for all of our deployed forces who are out there doing our nation's work, and sir, with that I'll kick it back over to you. Very good. We'll take a few questions. Go ahead. Thank you. Alexandra Ingersol, One America News. Do you assess, Mr. Secretary, do you assess what's left of this small boat fleet to be a significant threat or a nuisance to be managed? And then secondly, what is your message to critics who say that the US doesn't have a strategy in this mission? Well, any threat needs to be taken seriously, and just like those six attack boats that the Chairman mentioned were taken seriously and dealt with before they were any real threat to the American military vessels that they were approaching. And that is—small craft like that are all that Iran has left. Their ability to get close with a destroyer of the capabilities that we have is limited, but we're going to take it very seriously and kinetically quickly. We're not going to allow a threat to gather. And I can tell you, even from just this morning, the strategy remains laser-focused. In fact, what I think you see from Project Freedom is that we're not allowing ourselves to get distracted. This is a separate and distinct effort, temporary in nature, that we plan to hand over to the world. The world has expressed a desire to be a part of this, as is often the case, or maybe almost always the case, American leadership is required, so the President was willing to undertake this, send commercial ships through, send destroyers in, provide this red, white, and blue bubble of protection, and encourage the world to step up because ultimately this waterway is, as I said, far more crucial to the rest of the world, and they need to have the ability to defend it. LIVE: Marco Rubio Holds White House Briefing After U.S. & Iran Exchange Fire In Strait Of Hormuz

Forbes Breaking News(5.5M)·88:51·13.2K views·2026-05-05
Marco RubioSecretary of State
TL;DRSecretary of State Marco Rubio announced "Project Freedom," a U.S.-led military corridor designed to rescue 23,000 civilians stranded by Iran’s illegal blockade of the Strait of Hormuz.
Rubio warned that Iran faces total economic collapse, secondary sanctions on its...

TL;DR

Secretary of State Marco Rubio announced "Project Freedom," a U.S.-led military corridor designed to rescue 23,000 civilians stranded by Iran’s illegal blockade of the Strait of Hormuz. Rubio warned that Iran faces total economic collapse, secondary sanctions on its global partners, and decisive military deterrence if it does not abandon its nuclear weapons program and cease regional aggression.

***

Project Freedom and the Strait of Hormuz Blockade

  • The Rescue Mission: The U.S. military has launched Project Freedom to extract nearly 23,000 commercial crew members and civilians from 87 nations currently trapped in the Persian Gulf.
      • Stranded commercial crews have faced severe food and water shortages for over two months under the threat of Iranian attacks.
  • U.S. Military Deployment: The U.S. is establishing a protective naval and aerial "bubble" to escort merchant vessels through the strait.
      • The operation utilizes guided-missile destroyers, over 100 aircraft, unmanned systems, and 15,000 U.S. service members.
      • Two U.S.-flagged merchant ships have successfully transited the corridor.
      • U.S. forces have already destroyed seven Iranian fast boats, with orders to use lethal force only if actively attacked.
  • Countering "Act of War" Claims: Rubio forcefully rejected criticism from some members of Congress that the U.S. counter-blockade of Iranian shipping is an act of war.
      • He argued that Iran’s mining of international waters is the true illegal act of war, and the U.S. blockade of Iranian ships is a defensive counter-measure to prevent Iran from normalizing shipping tolls or lane closures.

Operation Economic Fury and Sanctions Leverage

  • Crippling Economic Damage: While the active combat phase of Operation Economic Fury has concluded, intense economic pressure continues to devastate the Iranian regime.
      • Iranian inflation has spiked to 70%, its currency is in free fall, and the blockade paired with U.S. sanctions has halted 90% of Iranian trade, costing the regime up to $500 million daily.
  • Secondary Sanctions Warning: The U.S. Department of the Treasury is actively identifying and blocking all sources of Iranian revenue.
      • Global Financial Consequences: Any foreign financial institution or commercial entity that assists Iran in evading sanctions will face immediate secondary sanctions and lose complete access to the U.S. financial system.
  • Degraded Military Capabilities: Rubio stated that the military phase of Operation Economic Fury successfully dismantled Iran’s conventional defense shield.
      • Iran's navy has been reduced to small boats, its air force is entirely inactive, and its missile-launching infrastructure and defense industrial base have been "severely damaged."

Nuclear Deterrence and Diplomatic Demands

  • The Danger of a Nuclear Iran: Rubio argued that allowing Iran to acquire nuclear weapons would permanently jeopardize global commerce.
      • If Iran possessed a nuclear weapon, it could close global shipping lanes at will without fear of international military retaliation.
      • Rubio pointed out that Iran's enrichment of uranium to 60% and its hidden, deep-mountain centrifuge facilities have absolutely zero legitimate civilian utility.
  • Diplomatic Strategy: Trump administration negotiators "Steve and Jared" are exploring potential diplomatic pathways, but the U.S. demands immediate, upfront Iranian concessions regarding nuclear materials before negotiations can proceed.
  • Fractured Leadership: U.S. efforts to negotiate are severely hampered by fractures within the Iranian government, where more practical civilian officials are at odds with radical clerics and Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps (IRGC) leaders.

Regional Geopolitics: China, Lebanon, and Cuba

  • China's Economic Vulnerability: Rubio emphasized that as an export-driven economy, China is directly harmed by Iran’s disruption of global shipping lanes.
      • While Beijing has instructed domestic firms to ignore U.S. sanctions, Rubio warned they will face strict Treasury enforcement.
      • President Trump intends to raise human rights, religious freedom, and Taiwan during his upcoming bilateral meeting with Chinese President Xi Jinping.
  • Lebanon and Hezbollah: Rubio asserted that peace between Israel and Lebanon is entirely feasible, but is actively blocked by Hezbollah, which operates as an armed extension of Tehran.
      • The U.S. seeks to bolster the capability of the Lebanese Armed Forces to disarm Hezbollah and stabilize the country.
  • Cuba's Energy Crisis: Rubio cleared up misconceptions about a U.S. oil blockade on Cuba, explaining that Cuba's fuel crisis is due to Venezuela halting its free oil shipments.
      • The U.S. offered $6 million in humanitarian aid to the Cuban people to be distributed through the Catholic Church, but the Cuban government has blocked the aid.

Executive Authority and the War Powers Act

  • Constitutional Position: Rubio reiterated the administration's firm stance that the War Powers Act is entirely unconstitutional.
      • While the White House complies with congressional notification requirements to maintain good legislative relations, it does not recognize the Act as a legitimate check on the President's constitutional authority as Commander-in-Chief.

***

Notable Quotes

"Under no circumstances can we ever allow them to normalize the fact that they get to blow up commercial ships and put mines in the water... That's not an act of war, that's a defensive measure, it's a counter to what they have decided to do." — Secretary of State Marco Rubio
"A nuclear-armed Iran could do whatever the hell they want with the straits and there's nothing anyone would be able to do about it... They would do exactly to the world with a nuclear weapon what they're doing now with the straits." — Secretary of State Marco Rubio
"They should check themselves before they wreck themselves in the direction that they're going." — Secretary of State Marco Rubio
"Even as a Senator, I said something. The War Powers Act is unconstitutional. One hundred percent... We don't acknowledge the law as constitutional." — Secretary of State Marco Rubio

For over two months, commercial crew members have faced shortages of food and water under threat from Iranian attacks. The U.S. military is providing a defensive bubble to guide stranded ships safely, responding with lethal force only if attacked. So far, two U.S.-flagged merchant ships have safely crossed. WATCH: Vice President JD Vance delivers remarks at Iowa campaign event

Fox News(15.3M)·36:02·33.5K views·2026-05-05
JD VanceVice President Zach NunnUS Representative, Iowa
TL;DRVice President JD Vance framed the upcoming 2026 elections as a fundamental choice between a government that prioritizes American citizens and workers through "common sense" economic protectionism and anti-fraud measures, or one that favors special interests and illegal immigrants.

TL;DR

Vice President JD Vance framed the upcoming 2026 elections as a fundamental choice between a government that prioritizes American citizens and workers through "common sense" economic protectionism and anti-fraud measures, or one that favors special interests and illegal immigrants. Rallying for Representative Zach Nunn, Vance highlighted the administration's focus on Iowa agriculture, domestic manufacturing, and fiscal accountability.

Economic Protectionism and Manufacturing

  • Support for Domestic Industry: Vance shared a narrative of an Iowa factory nearly driven out of business by Chinese "dumping" and slave labor, contrasting this with the administration’s current trade stance.
      • Tariff Policy: Stressed that foreign countries attempting to undercut Iowa workers must pay a "big fat tariff" to protect domestic jobs.
      • Tax Incentives: Credited the Working Families Tax Cuts, supported by Rep. Zach Nunn, for allowing businesses to increase bonuses, salaries, and staffing.
  • Housing and Foreign Investment: Linked the rising cost of living to foreign and corporate ownership of American assets.
      • Prioritizing Families: Argued that American homes should belong to families rather than foreign investors or Chinese entities buying farmland.
      • Immigration Link: Suggested that housing costs are exacerbated by the presence of millions of illegal immigrants and called for border security as a primary tool for lowering rent.

Federal Oversight and the Fraud Task Force

  • Eradicating Government Waste: As leader of the federal fraud task force, Vance emphasized that taxpayer dollars must be protected from systemic abuse.
      • SNAP Benefits Abuse: Reported that Agriculture Secretary Brooke Rollins identified 186,000 deceased individuals and 355,000 people receiving double benefits under the SNAP program.
      • Subpoena Power: Confirmed that the task force served 22 investigatory subpoenas to the Department of Justice in just three months to prosecute fraudsters.
  • Targeting Welfare Fraud: Highlighted a specific case in Minneapolis where funds intended for parents of children with autism were allegedly diverted to "Somalian fraudsters" through identity fraud.
      • Federal Audits: Noted that the administration is threatening to cut off federal funding to states that refuse to audit benefit recipients to confirm eligibility.

Agriculture and Trade Expansion

  • Market Access: Claimed the administration has doubled the export market for Iowa farmers in the last 18 months by using trade authorities to force foreign countries to accept U.S. agricultural products.
  • Biofuels and Energy:
      • E15 Support: Voiced strong support for Rep. Zach Nunn’s legislation to expand the sale of E15 fuel nationwide to benefit Iowa corn growers.
      • Input Costs: Acknowledged the struggle with high fertilizer prices and committed to finding ways to lower these costs for the farming community.

Political Contrast and Campaign Strategy

  • Demographic Shift: Vance, citing his own upbringing in a "union Democrat" family, argued that the modern Democratic Party has abandoned working people in favor of social issues.
  • Legislative Critique: Attacked opponent Sarah Trone Garret’s voting record, specifically regarding gender transition surgeries for minors and biological males in women's sports.
  • The "Common Sense" Mandate: Defined the Republican platform as a return to simple principles: "American government ought to be fighting for America's citizens rather than illegal aliens."
  • Honoring Sacrifice: Closed with a reflection on meeting Gold Star families in Des Moines, arguing that responsible governance is a way to "earn" the ultimate sacrifice made by members of the military.
"Finding fraud in the federal government, it's kind of like fishing in a barrel with dynamite... I am shocked every single day by the things that we find." — JD Vance
"We have two parties in Washington DC... it's a heartbreaking thing for a kid who came from a union Democrat family to realize that Democrats these days, they seem to care more about gender transition than they do about you keeping more of your hard-earned money." — JD Vance
"Part of how we earn that incredible sacrifice given to all of us is by making this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again." — JD Vance

But she had survived. Miraculously, she was in amazing condition. She was a sweet, really cute kid, and you know, I'm the father of a six-year-old boy. He's actually here with me tonight; he's backstage. And this girl was so proud. She was proud to be there in the chamber and she gives her dad a big hug, and the Republicans all stand and cheer, and the Democrats all sit on their hands. Booo! I remember thinking to myself, "What is wrong with you that you cannot stand up and cheer for a six-year-old girl who survived an assassin's bullet?" What is wrong with you that you cannot vote to give more money to the pockets of Iowa farmers and Iowa factory workers? What is wrong with you when you cannot stand up for the Americans, some of whom literally have taken bullets in the United States of America, but you fight every single day for illegal immigrants who have no right to be in the United States in the first place? And what does it say about a political party that they have fought more against our anti-fraud efforts than they ever did to protect your dollars and to protect the benefits of the people who use those benefits? My friends, this is not a normal election; this is not a normal political environment. This is a contest between a party that wants to take all of your money and give it to illegal aliens and a contest between gentlemen like Zach Nunn who fight every single day for you. And I have a simple question here, which is: do you want somebody who votes to give your money to illegal aliens? No! Do you want somebody who votes to raise your taxes? No! Do you want somebody who supports defrauding you and taking money away from poor kids so they can give it to the fraudsters? No! Then do we want crazy far-left Democrats in Washington, D.C.? No! Here's what we do want. Do we want somebody who fights for you every single day? Yes! Do we want somebody who has put more money in your pocket? Yes! Do we want somebody who gives E15 all over the United States of America so Iowa farmers can profit from it? Yes! So what do we want? We want Congressman Zach Nunn, and you gotta get him to Washington, D.C.! God bless you. God bless you. No, please. So let me just say one more thing, my friends, and then I will hit the road. You know, like I said, I've got my six-year-old son back there. And the backstory of why he’s here—by the way, I started in Washington, D.C., we flew from Washington to Ohio, and I voted in Ohio's primary today. From Ohio, that's right. The media asked me who I voted for. None of your business. We went from Ohio to Oklahoma City to do a fundraiser for the Republican National Committee, and then I came here to be with all of you this evening. And you know, I can't wait to tell my wife when we get home that we've watched about nine episodes of X-Men and my son has eaten four chocolate chip cookies. She's going to be very pleased with the Vice President. But here's the thing. I didn't plan this, but I've got my six-year-old because last week I took his little sister on a trip and he was feeling a little jealous. You know, when he's a kindergartner, it's not like he misses school—no offense—but one day of kindergarten's not gonna cause him any problems. So he came out with me today and we've had such a good day; it’s been an amazing thing. I always enjoy coming out and doing events like this, but to do it with your six-year-old son by your side is really an amazing thing. When we landed here at the airport in Des Moines, we met a couple of Gold Star families from Iowa. And a couple of you probably know this—maybe all of you know this—that in what's going on in the Middle East, with this operation in Iran, Iowa has borne a heavier burden maybe than any other state in the union. This great state has lost about half of our KIA, and I know that you all will join me in saying that we love them and we're proud of them and we're praying for them every single day. Also on the tarmac, a couple of families who've lost people just in the last nine or so months met me—one in Iran and one in Syria. I was talking to them, and one of them told me—I had no idea, I didn't plan to see them but they were here and of course I was honored to see them. It's an amazing thing as a Vice President of the United States to meet the parents and the families of the people who put on a uniform and sacrificed their life for this country. I'm always happy to do it, always honored to do it. But one family—and I won't use their name, I don't know how political they are if they're political at all—they told me that their son's birthday was today. And so I get in the car with my little six-year-old, and I look into those big eyes—his eyes remind me of his mother's eyes—and I think to myself, "What an amazing blessing it is to be a father in the freest and most prosperous country anywhere in the history of the world." I thought to myself: what would I say if this beautiful six-year-old boy got older and decided, like his dad, to put on the uniform of his country? And I thought to myself, on the one hand, I'd be so proud of him, but on the other hand, I'd be so terrified that what happened to those two families would happen to this boy. It hit me that every time we lose somebody, every time somebody goes overseas and sacrifices their life, every time that a person gives the ultimate sacrifice to the United States of America, we often read about it as a line in a newspaper or online. But there's a father, a mother, a grandma, aunts, uncles, and a whole crew of people who love them the same way that we all love every single member of our family. You take that love and you set that on one side, and you consider the balance that all of us owe. Because on the other side, we have to meet their sacrifice by carrying something forward that they can't carry forward. We have to make this country worthy of that sacrifice. You remember that movie *Saving Private Ryan*? It's one of my favorite movies. At the very end, right before one of the soldiers takes his last breath, he looks up and he says, "Earn this." And what he means is, all that love, all that was taken away from those families, all that was taken away from so many of the people who have put on the uniform and sacrificed for this country—we have to earn it. Now, so much of that is how you live your life. So much of that is Congressman Zach Nunn being a good husband and father in his beautiful family here. I think what you guys have, six or seven? Six. She is a saint, Zach, she is a saint. Part of that is how we go to work and treat our employees and what we build and make with our hands and with our minds. Part of it is how we go to church and give back to our community. But part of how we earn that incredible sacrifice given to all of us is by making this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again. Part of what we have to do, my friends, is every single day we have to send people to Washington. I'm not saying you have to agree with every single issue. I'm saying that you gotta send people to Washington who wake up every single day and recognize that they fight for you. That's how we honor this sacrifice, that's how we make this country great again, and that's how we make 250 years of American history and American patriots proud. God bless you guys and thank you for having me in Iowa.

WATCH: VP Vance gives remarks in Des Moines, IA

LiveNOW from FOX(5.6M)·36:15·10.7K views·2026-05-05

a Democrat party he...

TL;DR

Vice President JD Vance advocated for the re-election of Congressman Zach Nunn, framing the 2026 election as a fundamental choice between a government that prioritizes American workers through manufacturing protection and anti-fraud measures versus a Democrat party he characterizes as prioritizing illegal immigration and corporate corruption.

Economic Growth and Manufacturing Protection

  • Domestic Tax Policy: Vance highlighted the "Working Families" tax cuts as a primary driver for local business expansion.
      • According to factory owners, these tax breaks allowed for higher bonuses, increased salaries, and the creation of new jobs in the Des Moines area.
  • Trade and Tariffs: The Vice President emphasized a "common sense" approach to trade that penalizes foreign "dumping."
      • The China Factor: Vance criticized past administrations for allowing China to use "slave labor" to undercut Iowa workers.
      • Tariff Strategy: He reaffirmed the administration's stance that foreign countries attempting to steal American jobs must pay a "big fat tariff" to access U.S. markets.
  • Housing and Cost of Living: Vance claimed that for the first time in five years, rent costs have decreased for eight consecutive months.
      • Policy Drivers: He attributed this shift to principles favoring American family homeownership over foreign investors and "Chinese investors buying up farmland."
      • Immigration Link: He argued that sealing the border would lower housing costs by reducing the demand for 30 million homes currently occupied by illegal immigrants.

Federal Accountability and the Fraud Task Force

  • Anti-Fraud Initiatives: As the leader of the federal fraud task force, Vance described the government as "fishing in a barrel with dynamite" regarding the discovery of misappropriated funds.
  • SNAP Program Abuse: Agriculture Secretary Brooke Rollins has identified significant mismanagement within the Supplemental Nutrition Assistance Program (SNAP).
      • Fact: 186,000 deceased individuals are currently receiving food stamps.
      • Fact: 355,000 people are receiving double benefits.
      • Wealth Disparity: Investigations found individuals owning luxury vehicles, such as Lamborghinis, while remaining on the SNAP rolls.
  • International Fraud: Vance detailed a case in Minneapolis where funds intended for parents of children with autism were diverted to "Somalian fraudsters" via illegal immigrant networks.
      • The Federal Response: The administration has threatened to cut off federal funding to states like Minnesota unless they conduct rigorous audits of benefit recipients.

Agricultural Expansion and Biofuels

  • Export Market Growth: Vance reported that the administration has doubled the export market for Iowa farmers in just 18 months.
      • This was achieved by leveraging trade authorities to demand market access for Iowa products in exchange for lower tariffs on foreign goods.
  • Energy Independence (E15): The Vice President pledged continued support for Congressman Nunn’s legislation to expand E15 ethanol access nationwide.
      • Goals: Increasing profit margins for Iowa farmers while lowering fuel costs for consumers across all 50 states.
  • Input Costs: Acknowledged the strain of high fertilizer prices and committed to working on domestic supply chain solutions to alleviate these costs for farmers.

Political Contrast and "Earning the Sacrifice"

  • Congressional Matchup: Vance contrasted Congressman Zach Nunn with his opponent, Sarah Trone Garriott, focusing on their legislative priorities.
      • He criticized Garriott’s voting record on social issues—such as gender transition for minors and transgender participation in sports—arguing these topics distract from the economic needs of the district.
  • Party Realignment: Vance, who noted he was raised in a "union Democrat" household, argued the modern Democrat party has abandoned working-class families in favor of "insider stock trading" and illegal immigrant advocacy.
  • The "Earn This" Standard: Referencing a meeting with Gold Star families in Des Moines, Vance closed with a call to make the government worthy of the ultimate sacrifice made by service members.
      • The Burden of Service: He noted that Iowa has borne a heavy burden in recent Middle East operations, losing a significant percentage of those killed in action.
      • Political Duty: He defined "earning" that sacrifice as sending representatives to Washington who prioritize the American citizen's "sweat, tears, and time."

Notable Quotes

"Do you want people in Washington, D.C. who fight for you, who fight for the people of this district, or who fight for corruption and fraud?" — Vice President JD Vance
"Finding fraud in the federal government—it's kind of like fishing in a barrel with dynamite." — Vice President JD Vance
"I actually think that we should take food stamps away from dead people. I am guilty of that. I think that's a reasonable thing." — Vice President JD Vance
"Part of how we earn that incredible sacrifice given to all of us is by making this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again." — Vice President JD Vance

That's what he's been doing. Now let me just give you a very concrete example of what fighting for you looks like. This is not just abstract; this is not words written on a paper. Bring those things that were built by hands of slaves rather than the hands of our own workers." By the time I graduated from high school, the manufacturers were laying people off. Those big, beautiful factories were shuttering their doors. It's heartbreaking for a kid who came from a union Democrat family to realize that Democrats these days seem to care more about gender transition than they do about you keeping more of your hard-earned money. I really do believe this: there are Democrats like my mamaw and papaw all over the great state of Iowa, but I hate to say it and I hate to break it to you, but there are none left in Washington, D.C. The Democrats in Washington, D.C. want to trade stocks—insider trading for money—just like Nancy Pelosi did. The best part of the State of the Union address was when the President of the United States called out Nancy Pelosi for her stock trading. I looked over at her and she had the sourest look I have ever seen on a human being's face. It turns out Nancy Pelosi likes nothing less than being called out for her insider stock trading. You know, we were just talking about that at the State of the Union. We had this beautiful six-year-old girl—you may remember this, it was a few months ago, but it was a very revealing moment about who our respective political parties stand for. This little girl had been shot by an illegal alien. But she had survived; miraculously, she was in amazing condition. She was a sweet, just a really cute kid. And you know, I'm the father of a six-year-old boy; he's actually here with me, he's backstage. This girl was so proud. She was proud to be there in the chamber and she gave her dad a big hug, and the Republicans all stood and cheered, and the Democrats all sat on their hands. I remember thinking to myself: what is wrong with you that you cannot stand up and cheer for a six-year-old girl who survived an assassin's bullet? What is wrong with you that you cannot vote to give more money to the pockets of Iowa farmers and Iowa factory workers? What is wrong with you when you cannot stand up for the Americans—some of whom literally have taken bullets in the United States of America—but you fight every single day for illegal immigrants who have no right to be in the United States in the first place? And what does it say about a political party that they have fought more against our anti-fraud efforts than they ever did to protect your dollars and to protect the benefits of the people who use them? My friends, this is not a normal election. This is not a normal political environment. This is a contest between a party that wants to take all of your money and give it to illegal aliens and a contest between gentlemen like Zach Nunn who fight every single day for you. I have a simple question here: do you want somebody who votes to give your money to illegal aliens? No! Do you want somebody who votes to raise your taxes? No! Do you want somebody who supports defrauding you and taking money away from poor kids so they can give it to the fraudsters? No! Then do we want crazy far-left Democrats in Washington, D.C.? No! Here's what we do want. Do we want somebody who fights for you every single day? Yes! Do we want somebody who has put more money in your pocket? Yes! Do we want somebody who gives E15 all over the United States of America so Iowa farmers can profit from it? Yes! So what do we want? We want Congressman Zach Nunn, and you've got to get him to Washington, D.C. So let me just say one more thing, my friends, and then I will hit the road. Like I said, I've got my six-year-old son back there. And the backstory of why I started in Washington, D.C.—we flew from Washington to Ohio. I voted in Ohio's primary today. That's right. The media asked me who I voted for—none of your business! Went from Ohio to Oklahoma City to do a fundraiser for the Republican National Committee and then I came here to be with all of you this evening. I can't wait to tell my wife when we get home that we've watched about nine episodes of X-Men and my son has eaten four chocolate chip cookies. She's going to be very pleased; she's going to be very pleased with the vice president. But here's the thing: it kind of just worked out. I wasn't planning this, but I've got my six-year-old because last week I took his little sister on a trip and he was feeling a little jealous. You know, when he's a kindergartener, it's not like missing school—no offense—but one day of kindergarten is not going to cause him any problems. So he came out with me today and we've had such a good day. It's just been an amazing thing. I always enjoy coming out and doing events like this, but to do it with your six-year-old son by your side is really an amazing thing. But as it happened, when we landed here in Des Moines at the airport, we met a couple of Gold Star families from Iowa. A couple of you probably know this—maybe all of you know this—that in what's going on in the Middle East, this operation in Iran, Iowa has borne a heavier burden maybe than any other state in the Union. This great state has lost about half of our KIA, and I know that you all will join me in saying that we love them, and we're proud of them, and we're praying for them every single day. Thank you. On the tarmac, a couple of Gold Star families met me—a couple of families who've lost people just in the last nine or so months. One in Iran and then one in Syria about nine or so months ago. I was talking to them and one of them told me—I had no idea, I didn't plan to see them—but they were here and of course I was honored to see them. It's an amazing thing as the Vice President of the United States to meet the parents and the families of the people who put on a uniform and sacrificed their lives for this country. I'm always happy to do it, always honored to do it. But one family—and I won't use their name, I don't know how political they are, if they're political at all—told me that their son's birthday was today. And so I get in the car with my little six-year-old and I look into those big eyes—his eyes remind me of his mother's eyes—and I think to myself: what an amazing blessing it is to be able to be a father in the freest and most prosperous country anywhere in the history of the world. I thought to myself: what would I say if this beautiful six-year-old boy got older and decided, like his dad, to put on the uniform of his country and, like so many of you here, decided to put on the uniform of his country? On the one hand, I'd be so proud of him. I'd be so proud of him. But on the other hand, I'd be so terrified that what happened to those two families would happen to this boy. It hit me that every time we lose somebody, every time someone goes overseas and sacrifices their life, every time that a person gives the ultimate sacrifice to the United States of America, we often read about it as a line in a newspaper or online. But there's a father, and there's a mother, and there's a grandma, and aunts and uncles, and a whole crew of people who love them the same way that we all love every single member of our family. You take that love and you set that on one side, and you consider the balance that all of us owe. On the other side is that we have to meet their sacrifice by carrying something forward that they can't carry forward. We have to make this country worthy of that sacrifice. You remember that movie *Saving Private Ryan*? That's one of my favorite movies. At the very end, right before one of the soldiers takes his last breath, he looks up and he says, "Earn this." What he means is all that love, all that was taken away from those families, all that was taken away from so many of the people who have put on the uniform and sacrificed for this country—we have to earn it. So much of that is how you live your life. So much of that is, you know, Congressman Zach Nunn being a good husband and father in his beautiful family here. I think—what, you guys have six or seven? Six. She is a saint, Zach. She is a saint. Part of that is how we go to work and treat our employees and what we build and make with our hands and with our minds. Part of it is how we go to church and give back to our community. But part of how we earn that incredible sacrifice given to all of us is by making this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again. Part of what we have to do, my friends, is every single day we have to send people to Washington—I'm not saying you have to agree with every single issue—I'm saying that you've got to send people to Washington who wake up every single day and recognize that they fight for you. That's how we honor this sacrifice. That's how we make this country great again. And that's how we make 250 years of American history and American patriots proud. God bless you guys and thank you for having me in Iowa.

Vice President JD Vance Delivers Remarks in Des Moines, Iowa

markets, and a new federal...

TL;DR

Vice President JD Vance and Congressman Zach Nunn met with manufacturing leaders in Des Moines to promote "America First" economic policies, highlighting the fight against Chinese intellectual property theft, the expansion of agricultural export markets, and a new federal crackdown on government fraud.

Manufacturing and Trade Accountability

  • Combatting Industrial Espionage: Congressman Nunn highlighted the host venue, X-Guard, as a victim of intellectual property theft.
      • He alleged that Beijing "poached" American designs for tractor-trailer safety equipment and "dumped" the copied products back into the U.S. market to undercut domestic manufacturing.
  • Tariff Policy: Vice President Vance emphasized that current trade policy focuses on protecting American wages through "big fat tariffs" on foreign countries that utilize cheap or slave labor.
      • The administration’s stance is that domestic builders deserve tax cuts, while those dumping goods into the U.S. market should pay a premium to enter.
  • Domestic Success: X-Guard owners reported that tax cuts for working families directly allowed for higher worker bonuses and business expansion.

Agricultural Priorities and Rural Infrastructure

  • The Farm Bill: Congressman Nunn discussed the recent bipartisan movement of a Farm Bill that includes 21 specific Iowa priorities.
      • Biofuels: Legislation is moving forward to enable year-round, nationwide sales of E15 fuel.
      • Connectivity: A focus on rural broadband to support telehealth and autonomous farming technology.
      • Livestock Protections: Efforts to end animal torture and "puppy mills" by mirroring state-level legislation at the federal level.
  • Market Expansion: Vance reported that trade policies have doubled the export market for Iowa farmers in the last 18 months.
      • The administration used trade authorities to force foreign countries to stop dumping agricultural products and instead open their borders to U.S.-grown goods.

Federal Oversight and Government Reform

  • The Fraud Task Force: Vice President Vance, leading a federal fraud task force, reported significant findings in the SNAP (food stamps) program.
      • Specific Findings: Discoveries include 186,000 deceased individuals and 355,000 people receiving double benefits.
      • Enforcement: Vance noted the issuance of 22 investigative subpoenas in Minneapolis and stated that those defrauding the government will face prison time.
  • Legislative Ethics: Congressman Nunn advocated for the "Stock Act" to end insider trading among members of Congress.
      • He cited $200 million in stock trades by Congressional members in the last year as evidence of the need for reform, alongside proposals for term limits.

Economic Policy and National Security

  • Housing Affordability: Vance linked the rising cost of housing to foreign investment and illegal immigration.
      • He argued that by sealing the border and preventing foreign entities (specifically Chinese investors) from buying up farmland and residential homes, supply will return to American families.
  • Veterans and Gold Star Families: Both speakers addressed the disproportionate sacrifice of Iowa service members.
      • Vance emphasized a moral obligation to "earn" the sacrifice of fallen soldiers by ensuring the federal government remains worthy of their service and focused on its own citizens first.

Notable Quotes

"Our tax policy ought to be pretty simple... If you're building right here in Iowa... you deserve a tax cut. But if you're a foreign country dumping that garbage into our country... you're going to pay a big fat tariff." — Vice President JD Vance
"Not only did they want to put Sam and Ryan out of business, they were trying to put an American industry to bed so they could own that space going forward. I’m so proud... of holding bad actors accountable." — Congressman Zach Nunn
"We have to make this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again." — Vice President JD Vance

That foreign countries, in particular the People's Republic of China, was dumping goods, undercutting the wages of the workers of this factory, and driving this place out of business. They were using cheap labor, sometimes slave labor, to try to steal jobs from the hardworking people of this district and this factory floor. Bring those things that were built by hands of slaves rather than the hands of our own workers." The factories closed down. Those big, beautiful factories were shuttering their doors. And we never had a political movement that said enough is enough until Donald J. Trump and Zach Nunn came along. And you know what we said? The Democrats every day, they will tell you they will fight against our policies to try to bring back American manufacturing. They will fight against our policies that try to fight back against those people who would dump that stuff into our communities. And you know what we say? We say that our tax policy ought to be pretty simple, and that's exactly what it has been. If you're building right here in Iowa, if you're making something right here in Iowa, if you're working every single day right here in Iowa, you deserve a tax cut and that's exactly what we delivered with Congressman Nunn. But if you're a foreign country dumping that garbage into our country, if you're trying to undercut the wages of Iowa workers, if you're trying to steal the jobs from Iowa farmers and Iowa manufacturers, you know what you're going to do? You're going to pay a big fat tariff before you bring anything into our country because we're protecting the jobs of our workers and our people for a change. And that's all this is about. When you hear the Democrats attack the Trump administration's tax policies, that's what they're attacking. They're attacking the policies that make it harder for people to steal your jobs and they're attacking the policies that give you more money to keep in your own pocket. Now I talked to the factory owners again just a couple of hours ago... couple of minutes ago, I should say. And you know what they told me? They told me that the working families tax cuts, the tax cuts made possible by Congressman Nunn, meant that their business had a lot more money that they could give to workers in higher bonuses and higher salaries. That they could hire more people, that they could expand and create new jobs that didn't exist before. Isn't it nice to have a government that finally is fighting for you instead of fighting against you? And that's what we're trying to have in Washington, DC. There is so much... so much I'm proud of, so much that is moving in the right direction. Do you know when I was going around the campaign trail in 2024, one of the number one things that young people said to me—young Americans in particular—is that they couldn't afford to buy a home. They couldn't afford their rent if that's what they wanted to do. And you know, for the first time in over five years, for eight months running, we have seen the cost of rent come down in the United States of America. Our young people are starting to get close; they're making progress. They're starting to get to the point where they could finally afford their slice of the American dream. And you know why we did that? And you know how we did it? It's actually not that complicated. A simple principle: American homes ought to belong to American families, not foreign investors, not foreign owners, and not Chinese investors who are buying up our farmland. Again, it's not rocket science; it's a simple principle that if you have a government that fights for you, it can make your life easier. It can make it easier for you to start a business or to work at an amazing job. We didn't do anything that was particularly difficult; we did something that was simple and common sense. And I think that's what defines the Republican Party in Washington right now: it's simply about common sense. You want to lower the cost of homes for American families? Here's a simple thing. Why don't you stop giving 30 million homes to illegal aliens? Why don't you seal the border and make sure those homes go to American families for a change? That's how you lower the cost of housing. If you want to make it easier for young Americans to start a family or to get a good job, stop giving jobs to foreign companies and stop giving jobs to foreign countries and protect the good well-paying jobs that exist right here in the United States of America, and that's what we did. And here's the final thing. When we talk about standing for you—again, whatever your views on a specific policy—there is maybe no more important issue than how about when you pay your taxes to the federal government. We just had tax day just a couple of weeks ago. How about you have a government that actually takes those resources as what they are: your sweat, your tears, your time away from your family, and protects every single one of those dollars. And that's what we're doing by going after fraud finally in the federal government. And it, ladies and gentlemen, people have asked me, "you know, I'm the leader of the fraud task force in Washington." And people have asked me, "is that a hard job?" And I say, well, let me think: finding fraud in the federal government is kind of like fishing in a barrel with dynamite. Every week I get a report from the task force—you know, we have our weekly meeting—and I am shocked every single day by the things that we find. Just one of the all-stars on our fraud task force is our great Agriculture Secretary, Brooke Rollins. And Brooke has found out that we've got 355,000 people on SNAP benefits receiving double benefits. We've got 186,000 dead people getting SNAP benefits. 186,000 dead Americans getting food stamps right now. Now, I know the fake news media is going to say that the big headline from this speech is "JD Vance proposes that we take away food stamps." That's what they're going to say. I actually think that we should take food stamps away from dead people. I am guilty of that. I think that's a reasonable thing. I also was talking to Brooke backstage and she said... she said, you know, that there are people who are... who have Lamborghinis. This is not a joke. There are people who have Lamborghinis who currently receive SNAP benefits. I said, "huh, that's interesting." You know, I'm a pretty conservative guy, but I would think that like 95% of the United States of America would agree that if you are wealthy enough to afford a Lamborghini, then you are wealthy enough to not receive SNAP benefits from the American people. Is that common sense? And I could go down and down the list. We just served 22 investigatory procedures with the Department of Justice. We went from discovering what happened in Minneapolis to serving 22, you know, subpoenas so that we could go after the fraud that's happening in Minneapolis. And we did that in just three months. And yes, ladies and gentlemen, when we find crime, those people are going to go to prison for defrauding you because that's exactly how it should be. Now the last thing I want to talk about, my friends, is we know that under the Biden administration, Iowa farmers and farmers all over the United States of America were hit and they were hit hard. What we've done using the President's trade authorities and using his incredible trade policies is that we have doubled the export market for Iowa farmers in just 18 months. And that is an amazing thing. Because what happened for years is that people would dump their agricultural products into the United States of America but said you're not allowed to sell great Iowa product overseas. Well, we flipped that on its head. We told all those countries: you're done dumping that crap into the United States of America and if you don't want to pay a higher tariff rate, you better let Iowa farmers sell into your country. And every single one of them has let Iowa farmers sell into their country. Again, it's amazing what happens when you've got a President and a Congressman who's fighting for you instead of fighting against you, and that is the record that we have had over the past 18 months. So let me... let me just say, let me say a couple more things here and then I will hit the road. You know I, like I said, I've got my six-year-old son back there. And the backstory, by the way, of why I started in Washington, DC... we flew from Washington to Ohio; I voted in Ohio's primary today. That's right. The media asked me who I voted for—none of your business. Went from Ohio to Oklahoma City to do a fundraiser for the Republican National Committee and then I came here to be with all of you this evening. And you know, I can't wait to tell my wife when we get home that we've watched about nine episodes of X-Men and my son has eaten four chocolate chip cookies. She's going to be very pleased with the Vice President. But here's the thing. It kind of just worked out—I wasn't planning this—but I've got my six-year-old because last week I took his little sister on a trip and he was feeling a little jealous. And you know, when he's a kindergartner it's not like missing school—no offense—but one day of kindergarten is not going to cause him any problems. So he came out with me today and we've had such a good day and it's just been an amazing thing. I always enjoy coming out and doing events like this, but to do it with your six-year-old son by your side is really an amazing and amazing thing. But as it happened, when we landed here in Des Moines, or at the airport there in Des Moines, we met a couple of Gold Star families from Iowa. And a couple of you probably know this, maybe all of you know this, that in you know what's going on in the Middle East, this operation in Iran, Iowa has borne a heavier burden maybe than any other state in the Union. This great state has lost about half of our KIA and I know that you all will join me in saying that we love them and we're proud of them and we're praying for them every single day. But also on the tarmac, a couple of Gold Star families met me—a couple of families who've lost people just in the last, you know, nine or so months. One in Iran and then one in Syria about nine or so months ago. And I was talking to them and one of them told me—I had no idea, I didn't you know, I didn't plan to see them but they were here and of course I was honored to see them. It's an amazing thing as a Vice President of the United States to meet the parents and the families of the people who put on a uniform and sacrifice their life for this country. And so I'm always happy to do it, always honored to do it. But one family—and I won't use their name, I don't know how political they are if they're political at all—but they told me that their son's birthday was today. And so I get in the car with my little six-year-old. You know, and I look into those big eyes... his eyes remind me of his mother's eyes, and I think to myself what an amazing blessing it is to be able to be a father in the freest and most prosperous country anywhere in the history of the world. And I thought to myself, what would I say? What would I say if this beautiful six-year-old boy got older and decided like his dad to put on the uniform of his country? And like so many of you here, decided to put on the uniform of his country? And I thought to myself: on the one hand, I'd be so proud of him. I'd be so proud of him, but on the other hand, I'd be so terrified that what happened to those two families would happen to this boy. And it hit me that every time we lose somebody, every time somebody goes overseas and sacrifices their life, every time that a person gives the ultimate sacrifice to the United States of America, we often read about it as a line in a newspaper or online. But there's a father and there's a mother and there's a grandma, aunts and uncles, and a whole crew of people who love them the same way that we all love every single member of our family. And you take that love and you set that on one side and you consider the balance that all of us owe. Because on the other side is we have to meet their sacrifice by carrying something forward that they can't carry forward. We have to make this country worthy of that sacrifice. You remember that movie Saving Private Ryan? It's one of my favorite movies. And at the very end, right before one of the soldiers takes his last breath, he looks up and he says, "earn this." And what he means is all that love, all that was taken away from those families, all that was taken away from so many of the people who have put on the uniform and sacrificed for this country, we have to earn it. Now so much of that is how you live your life. So much of that is, you know, Congressman Zach Nunn being a good husband and father in his beautiful family here. I think what you guys have, six or seven? Six. She is a saint, Zach, she is a saint. Part of that is how we go to work and treat our employees and what we build and make with our hands and with our minds. Part of that is how we go to church and give back to our community. But part of how we earn that incredible sacrifice given to all of us is by making this country's politics and government worthy of the people who put on the uniform and will never see their loved ones again. And part of what we have to do, my friends, is every single day we have to send people to Washington. I'm not saying you have to agree with every single issue; I am saying that you've got to send people to Washington who wake up every single day and recognize that they fight for you. That's how we honor this sacrifice. That's how we make this country great again and that's how we make 250 years of American history and American patriots proud. God bless you guys and thank you for having me in Iowa.

LIVE: VP Vance Speaks in Iowa

One America News Network(1.4M)·33:45·863 views·2026-05-05
JD VanceVice President
TL;DRVice President JD Vance’s address in Iowa frames the upcoming elections as a choice between "common sense" populist representation and a Democrat party he claims prioritizes illegal immigrants and foreign interests over American workers.
The briefing highlights aggressive...

TL;DR

Vice President JD Vance’s address in Iowa frames the upcoming elections as a choice between "common sense" populist representation and a Democrat party he claims prioritizes illegal immigrants and foreign interests over American workers. The briefing highlights aggressive anti-fraud initiatives, protectionist trade policies for Iowa farmers, and the re-election of Congressman Zach Nunn as the primary vehicle for this agenda.

Economic Protectionism and Manufacturing

  • Combating Foreign Trade Abuses: Vance emphasized a shift away from decades of "dumping" by the People's Republic of China, which he argues historically undercut Iowa wages and closed local factories.
      • Tariff Strategy: The administration utilizes "big fat tariffs" to protect domestic jobs, ensuring foreign competitors pay for market access while local manufacturers receive tax breaks.
  • Tax Policy Results: The Working Families Tax Cut is credited with providing businesses the capital to expand, increase salaries, and issue higher bonuses.
      • Direct Impact: Vance noted that since the administration took office, the average American family is reportedly $1,300 richer due to combined tax and housing policies.

Government Accountability and the National Fraud Task Force

  • Aggressive Oversight: As leader of the federal fraud task force, Vance described uncovering systemic corruption as "fishing in a barrel with dynamite."
  • SNAP Benefit Reform: Secretary of Agriculture Brooke Rollins identified significant misappropriation of food stamps, including:
      • Deceased Recipients: 186,000 dead individuals currently receiving benefits.
      • Benefit Doubling: 355,000 individuals receiving double SNAP benefits.
      • Wealth Disparity: Instances of individuals owning luxury vehicles (Lamborghinis) while remaining on the SNAP rolls.
  • Audit Enforcement: The administration has issued 22 subpoenas through the Department of Justice to investigate fraud, specifically citing a case in Minnesota where funds meant for autistic children were allegedly diverted to "Somalian fraudsters."

Housing and Border Security

  • Housing Affordability: Vance linked the high cost of rent and homeownership to foreign investment and illegal immigration.
      • Policy Principle: The administration advocates for the principle that "American homes belong to American families," not foreign investors or Chinese entities buying domestic farmland.
  • Supply and Demand: He argued that the housing crisis can be mitigated by ending the practice of providing housing to an estimated "30 million illegal aliens" and instead securing the border to stabilize costs for young citizens.

Iowa Agriculture and Local Representation

  • Market Expansion: Vance claimed that trade authorities have doubled the export market for Iowa farmers in the last 18 months by forcing foreign countries to accept Iowa products in exchange for US market access.
  • Energy Independence: He expressed strong support for E15 fuel, noting that Congressman Zach Nunn is currently advancing legislation to broaden its market reach.
  • Candidate Contrast: Vance sharply criticized Nunn’s opponent, Sarah Trone Garriott, for focusing on "far-left" social issues—such as gender transition policies in schools—rather than economic priorities like E15 expansion, fertilizer costs, or take-home pay.

National Service and Moral Obligations

  • Veterans and Gold Star Families: Reflecting on a meeting with families of service members killed in Iran and Syria, Vance argued that political leadership must be "worthy of the sacrifice" made by the military.
  • The "Earn This" Standard: Citing the film *Saving Private Ryan*, Vance stated that the primary duty of elected officials is to honor the fallen by waking up every day to fight for the American people’s interests rather than personal enrichment or insider trading.
